        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;

        }

        }

          width: 100%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);

          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

            width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Here is the situation:



<span class="line"><!---->Here is the situation:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





If the user submits an address, we will show a save dialog (currently rolled out to 20% stable to M94+). On Desktop that dialog has an edit button and if you *double* click (instead of single click) that button, we have a use after free. My non-security-expert impression would be that this is hard to exploit, but intuition is often wrong in security cases.



<span class="line"><!---->If the user submits an address, we will show a save dialog (currently rolled out to 20% stable to M94+). On Desktop that dialog has an edit button and if you *double* click (instead of single click) that button, we have a use after free. My non-security-expert impression would be that this is hard to exploit, but intuition is often wrong in security cases.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I would expect that the problem is triggered very rarely. Our metrics indicate that very few users press the edit button. 



<span class="line"><!---->I would expect that the problem is triggered very rarely. Our metrics indicate that very few users press the edit button. <!----></span>





https://uma.googleplex.com/p/chrome/histograms?sid=384fc6ccbe2b73fc44bc5c415551b978



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://uma.googleplex.com/p/chrome/histograms?sid=384fc6ccbe2b73fc44bc5c415551b978"><!---->https://uma.googleplex.com/p/chrome/histograms?sid=384fc6ccbe2b73fc44bc5c415551b978<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





Given that the dialog is pretty visible and already rolled out to 20%, the question is whether we have to roll back or fix forward.



<span class="line"><!---->Given that the dialog is pretty visible and already rolled out to 20%, the question is whether we have to roll back or fix forward.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





How would you feel about merging the fix to M97 for the first respin and once this is released, disable the feature on all previous versions?



<span class="line"><!---->How would you feel about merging the fix to M97 for the first respin and once this is released, disable the feature on all previous versions?<!----></span>

I just would like to clarify one thing.



<span class="line"><!---->I just would like to clarify one thing.<!----></span>



<br>





Here are the steps to exploit this bug:



<span class="line"><!---->Here are the steps to exploit this bug:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





- If the user submits an address, we will show a save dialog.



<span class="line"><!---->- If the user submits an address, we will show a save dialog.<!----></span>



<br>





- On Desktop that dialog has an edit button.



<span class="line"><!---->- On Desktop that dialog has an edit button.<!----></span>



<br>





- The user has to click the Edit dialog which open a modal dialog.



<span class="line"><!---->- The user has to click the Edit dialog which open a modal dialog.<!----></span>



<br>





- Another form submission needs to happen while the dialog is open (e.g. by some JavaScript).



<span class="line"><!---->- Another form submission needs to happen while the dialog is open (e.g. by some JavaScript).<!----></span>



<br>





- Another Save dialog is open with an Edit button.



<span class="line"><!---->- Another Save dialog is open with an Edit button.<!----></span>



<br>





- The user has to click the second Edit button (while the first is still open).



<span class="line"><!---->- The user has to click the second Edit button (while the first is still open).<!----></span>



<br>





- User-after-free happens when closing the tab.



<span class="line"><!---->- User-after-free happens when closing the tab.<!----></span>

Thanks for the question and insight in comments #19 and 20. Given this is an issue that results in browser process memory corruption, I'm not wild about letting it sit, but given this requires a fair amount user gesture (in terms of double/second clicks) as well as tab closure to trigger, I'm okay with not merging this back to M96, but the feature should be disabled on M96 as it will be Extended channel as M97 is stable. 



<span class="line"><!---->Thanks for the question and insight in comments #19 and 20. Given this is an issue that results in browser process memory corruption, I'm not wild about letting it sit, but given this requires a fair amount user gesture (in terms of double/second clicks) as well as tab closure to trigger, I'm okay with not merging this back to M96, but the feature should be disabled on M96 as it will be Extended channel as M97 is stable. <!----></span>



<br>





Please go ahead and merge to M97, branch 4758 as soon as possible. Thanks!



<span class="line"><!---->Please go ahead and merge to M97, branch 4758 as soon as possible. Thanks!<!----></span>

Dear owner, thanks for fixing this bug. We’ve reopened it because security bugs need Security_Severity and FoundIn labels set, which will enable the bots to request merges to the correct branches ( as well as helping out our vulnerability reward and CVE processes). Please consult with any Chrome security contact (

Please consult with any Chrome security contact (<!----></span>





security@chromium.org

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>
